pdef create_pipes

  ptrigger=0

end

;************************************************************


pdef control
  poffset=((1-poffset_marker)*plastoffset)+(poffset_marker*ip1)
  plastoffset=poffset

  pfeedback=plastout-(1*(ip1-ptarget-((1-zeroclamp)*poffset))/10000)
  pout=((1-pservo)*pfl)+(pservo*pfeedback)

  copy(pout,plastout,op1)
  copy(ptrigger,op0)

  merge(ip0,ip1,ip2,ip3,$binout)
end

;************************************************************


odef outputproc 2
  outputwait 2
  update burst
  set op0 a0
  set op1 a1
  time 500
end

;************************************************************

idef inputproc 4
  set ip0 s0
  set ip1 s1
  set ip2 s2
  set ip3 s3
  count 120000
  time 250
end

;************************************************************

start create_pipes,control,inputproc,outputproc
